class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n</div>\n<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of islands of Ireland</h1>\t\t\t<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">\n\t\t\t\t<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>\t\t\t\t<div id="contentSub"></div>\n\t\t\t\t<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>\t\t\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n\t\t\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>\n\t\t\t\t<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about offshore islands. For lake and river islands, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_inland_islands_of_Ireland" title="List of inland islands of Ireland">List of inland islands of Ireland</a>.</div>\n<table class="noprint infobox" id="GeoGroup" style="width: 23em; font-size: 88%; line-height: 1.5em">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<td><b>Map all coordinates using:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/osm4wiki/cgi-bin/wiki/wiki-osm.pl?project=en&amp;article=List_of_islands_of_Ireland">OpenStreetMap</a>&#160;\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Download coordinates as:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/kmlexport?article=List_of_islands_of_Ireland">KML</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://tripgang.com/kml2gpx/http%3A%2F%2Ftools.wmflabs.org%2Fkmlexport%3Farticle%3DList_of_islands_of_Ireland?gpx=1">GPX</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>This is a <b>list of islands of Ireland</b>. <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Ireland" title="Geography of Ireland">Ireland</a> is itself an island, lying west of the island of <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">Great Britain</a> and northwest of <a href="/wiki/Continental_Europe" title="Continental Europe">mainland Europe</a>. Islands are listed clockwise around the coast, starting from the north-east.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Hebrides" title="Hebrides">Hebrides</a> off <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Scotland" title="Geography of Scotland">Scotland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anglesey" title="Anglesey">Anglesey</a> off <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Wales" title="Geography of Wales">Wales</a> were grouped with Ireland ("<a href="/wiki/Hibernia" title="Hibernia">Hibernia</a>") by the <a href="/wiki/Greek_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Greek people">Greco</a>-<a href="/wiki/Ancient_Romans" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient Romans">Roman</a> <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Greek_geography" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient Greek geography">geographer</a> <a href="/wiki/Claudius_Ptolemy" class="mw-redirect" title="Claudius Ptolemy">Ptolemy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> but this is no longer common.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" data-sort-value="22" style="display:none;"></span>  c.22\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Total_population_of_Irish_offshore_Islands">Total population of Irish offshore Islands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_islands_of_Ireland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Total population of Irish offshore Islands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The number of people living on Irish islands decreased dramatically during the <a href="/wiki/Irish_famine" class="mw-redirect" title="Irish famine">Irish famine</a> and the period following it. Since then the trend on most islands has been a decreasing population until the 1950s and 1960s during which many islands were forcefully evacuated by the <a href="/wiki/Irish_Government" class="mw-redirect" title="Irish Government">Irish Government</a> as continuous bad weather meant that islanders were unable to travel to the mainland for several consecutive months. Of the remaining islands that weren\'t evacuated, many of their populations have continued to dwindle ever since, with some seeing stabilisation or even a slight uptick in population during and after the <a href="/wiki/Celtic_Tiger" title="Celtic Tiger">Celtic Tiger</a>.\n</p><p>The chart below shows the total number of people living on Irish islands throughout the years.\n</p>\n<table
